\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00039}00039     /**}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00048}00048 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00049}00049     /**}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00050}00050     Optional function that recomposes a multi-\/ROI frame into a displayable image buffer.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00051}00051     Every ROI will be copied into its appropriate location \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} the provided buffer.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00052}00052     Please note that the function will subtract the Implied ROI position \textcolor{keyword}{from} each ROI}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00053}00053     position which essentially moves the entire Implied ROI to a [0, 0] position.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00054}00054     Use the Offset arguments to shift all ROIs back to desired positions \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} needed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00055}00055     If you use the Implied ROI position \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} offset arguments the frame will be recomposed}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00056}00056     \textcolor{keyword}{as} it appears on the full frame.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00057}00057     The caller \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} responsible \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} black-\/filling the input buffer. Usually this function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00058}00058     \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} called during live/preview mode where the destination buffer \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} re-\/used. If the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00059}00059     ROIs do move during acquisition it \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} essential to black-\/fill the destination buffer}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00060}00060     before calling this function. This \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} \textcolor{keywordflow}{not} needed \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} the ROIs do \textcolor{keywordflow}{not} move.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00061}00061     If the ROIs move during live mode it \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} also recommended to use the offset arguments}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00062}00062     \textcolor{keywordflow}{and} recompose the ROI to a full frame -\/ \textcolor{keyword}{with} moving ROIs the implied ROI may change}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00063}00063     \textcolor{keyword}{with} each frame \textcolor{keywordflow}{and} this may cause undesired ROI \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}twitching"{}} \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} the displayable image.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00064}00064 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00065}00065     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} pDstBuf An output buffer, the buffer must be at least the size of the implied}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00066}00066                    ROI that \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} calculated during the frame decoding process. The buffer}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00067}00067                    must be of type uns16. If offset \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} set the buffer must be large}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00068}00068                    enough to allow the entire implied ROI to be shifted.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00069}00069     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} offX    Offset \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} the destination buffer, \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} pixels. If 0 the Implied}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00070}00070                    ROI will be shifted to position 0 \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} the target buffer.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00071}00071                    Use (ImpliedRoi.s1 / ImplierRoi.sbin) \textcolor{keyword}{as} offset value to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00072}00072                    disable the shift \textcolor{keywordflow}{and} keep the ROIs \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} their absolute positions.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00073}00073     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} offY    Offset \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} the destination buffer, \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} pixels. If 0 the Implied}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00074}00074                    ROI will be shifted to position 0 \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} the target buffer.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00075}00075                    Use (ImpliedRoi.p1 / ImplierRoi.pbin) \textcolor{keyword}{as} offset value to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00076}00076                    disable the shift \textcolor{keywordflow}{and} keep the ROIs \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} their absolute positions.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00077}00077     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} dstWidth  Width, \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} pixels of the destination image buffer. The buffer}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00078}00078                      must be large enough to hold the entire Implied ROI, including}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00079}00079                      the offsets (\textcolor{keywordflow}{if} used).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00080}00080     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} dstHeight Height, \textcolor{keywordflow}{in} pixels of the destination image buffer.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00081}00081     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} pSrcFrame A helper structure, previously decoded using the frame}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00082}00082                      decoding function.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00083}00083     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@return} \textcolor{comment}{\#PV\_FAIL in case of failure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00084}00084     */}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00085}00085     rs\_bool PV\_DECL pl\_md\_frame\_recompose (void* pDstBuf, uns16 offX, uns16 offY,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00086}00086                                            uns16 dstWidth, uns16 dstHeight,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00087}00087                                            md\_frame* pSrcFrame);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00088}00088 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00089}00089     /**}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00090}00090     This method creates an empty md\_frame structure \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} known number of ROIs.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00091}00091     Use this method to prepare \textcolor{keywordflow}{and} pre-\/allocate one structure before starting}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00092}00092     continous acquisition. Once callback arrives fill the structure \textcolor{keyword}{with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00093}00093     pl\_md\_frame\_decode() \textcolor{keywordflow}{and} display the metadata.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00094}00094     Release the structure when \textcolor{keywordflow}{not} needed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00095}00095     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} pFrame a pointer to frame helper structure address where the structure}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00096}00096                   will be allocated.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00097}00097     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} roiCount Number of ROIs the structure should be prepared \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00098}00098     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@return} \textcolor{comment}{\#PV\_FAIL in case of failure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00099}00099     */}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00100}00100     rs\_bool PV\_DECL pl\_md\_create\_frame\_struct\_cont (md\_frame** pFrame, uns16 roiCount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00101}00101 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00102}00102     /**}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00103}00103     This method creates an empty md\_frame structure \textcolor{keyword}{from} an existing buffer.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00104}00104     Use this method when loading buffers \textcolor{keyword}{from} disk \textcolor{keywordflow}{or} when performance \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} \textcolor{keywordflow}{not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00105}00105     critical. Do \textcolor{keywordflow}{not} forget to release the structure when \textcolor{keywordflow}{not} needed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00106}00106     For continous acquisition where the number \textcolor{keywordflow}{or} ROIs \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} known it \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} recommended}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00107}00107     to use the other provided method to avoid frequent memory allocation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00108}00108     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} pFrame A pointer address where the newly created structure will be stored.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00109}00109     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} pSrcBuf A raw frame data pointer \textcolor{keyword}{as} returned \textcolor{keyword}{from} the camera}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00110}00110     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@param} srcBufSize Size of the raw frame data buffer}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00111}00111     \textcolor{preprocessor}{@return} \textcolor{comment}{\#PV\_FAIL in case of failure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00112}00112     */}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{pvcam_8py_source_l00122}00122     /**}
